                     <div data-reactid="487">
                      <div data-reactid="488">
                       Kick the sand off your feet and relax in this charming Seaside cottage in the quiet Cove neighborhood away from the hubbub of downtown. Three blocks from the Promenade and beach, it's perfect for writers, artists, and peace-seekers. The cottage boasts modern comforts with a genuine midcentury feel. The space is open yet cozy, the bedrooms are comfortable and simple, and the kitchen is well-stocked for your beach getaway feasts. Enjoy happy hour at the picnic table on the front lawn!
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="489">
                       The cottage is a sweet, surprisingly open abode with an intentional combination of the original mid-century feel and the comforts you just want to have on a retreat at the beach. With 2 bedrooms (one king size bed, one queen size bed) that each boast big and bright windows to the spacious back yard and south morning sun, you will wake and sleep in comfort. You can enjoy the well-stocked kitchen prepared for meal making and coffee/tea drinking. The living space provides options for relaxation with two extremely comfy couches, a wood-burning fireplace, and Smart TV (if you so desire).
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="490">
                       A unique part of Seaside, the cottage is nestled within a residential neighborhood on the far south of town known by the locals as the Cove. Known for its quietness, isolation from the bulk of tourist activity, and inhabited by incredible neighbors (many year-round residents), the location can't be beat. The neighborhood offers the best of all worlds: privacy and peacefulness at the beach with quick access to the hype of downtown Seaside and Hwy 101 for day trip adventures.
                      </div>

The house has a beautiful view (pictures don't do it justice) and is very breezy; we kept the windows open most of the time because the weather was perfect. We would definitely stay here again.</p><span data-reactid="625">Jordan</span><span data-reactid="626">2015-07-06T00:00:00Z</span></li>

We were really careful with opening the TV cabinet and dresser drawers because they seemed delicate. We accidentally broke the $35 Chromecast because we couldn't see the cable (which was too short when the TV was extended, so it bent) and it wasn't clearly labeled from the front. We told her about it and sent a check to pay for this, as requested (after initially being told that it wasn't a big deal), which seemed a little awkward but understandable.
